  [user_task_description] # Requirements Document for 'EventPlanning' Web Application  ## 1. Objective Develop a comprehensive web application named 'EventPlanning' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to browse events, book tickets, view venue information, manage participants, and explore event schedules. No authentication required - all features are directly accessible. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.  ## 2. Language The required development language for the 'EventPlanning' application is Python.  ## 3. Page Design  The 'EventPlanning' web application will consist of the following eight pages:  ### 1. Dashboard Page - **Page Title**: Event Planning Dashboard - **Overview**: The main hub displaying upcoming events, featured venues, and quick navigation to all functionalities. - **Elements**:   - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.   - **ID: featured-events** - Type: Div - Display of featured event recommendations.   - **ID: browse-events-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to events listing page.   - **ID: view-tickets-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to tickets page.   - **ID: venues-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to venues page.  ### 2. Events Listing Page - **Page Title**: Events Catalog - **Overview**: A page displaying all available events with search and filter capabilities. - **Elements**:   - **ID: events-page** - Type: Div - Container for the events listing page.   - **ID: event-search-input** - Type: Input - Field to search events by name, location, or date.   - **ID: event-category-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by category (Conference, Concert, Sports, Workshop, Social).   - **ID: events-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying event cards with image, title, date, and location.   - **ID: view-event-button-{event_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view event details (each event card has this).  ### 3. Event Details Page - **Page Title**: Event Details - **Overview**: A page displaying detailed information about a specific event. - **Elements**:   - **ID: event-details-page** - Type: Div - Container for the event details page.   - **ID: event-title** - Type: H1 - Display event title.   - **ID: event-date** - Type: Div - Display event date and time.   - **ID: event-location** - Type: Div - Display event location.   - **ID: event-description** - Type: Div - Display detailed event description.   - **ID: book-ticket-button** - Type: Button - Button to book ticket for this event.  ### 4. Ticket Booking Page - **Page Title**: Book Your Tickets - **Overview**: A page for users to select and book tickets for events. - **Elements**:   - **ID: ticket-booking-page** - Type: Div - Container for the ticket booking page.   - **ID: select-event-dropdown** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select event to book tickets.   - **ID: ticket-quantity-input** - Type: Input (number) - Field to enter number of tickets.   - **ID: ticket-type-select** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select ticket type (General, VIP, Early Bird).   - **ID: book-now-button** - Type: Button - Button to proceed with ticket booking.   - **ID: booking-confirmation** - Type: Div - Display booking confirmation details.  ### 5. Participants Management Page - **Page Title**: Participants Management - **Overview**: A page for managing event participants and attendee lists. - **Elements**:   - **ID: participants-page** - Type: Div - Container for the participants management page.   - **ID: participants-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying participants with name, email, event, and status.   - **ID: add-participant-button** - Type: Button - Button to add new participant.   - **ID: search-participant-input** - Type: Input - Field to search participants by name or email.   - **ID: participant-status-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by status (Registered, Confirmed, Attended).  ### 6. Venue Information Page - **Page Title**: Venues - **Overview**: A page displaying available venues for events with detailed information. - **Elements**:   - **ID: venues-page** - Type: Div - Container for the venues page.   - **ID: venues-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying venue cards with name, capacity, and amenities.   - **ID: venue-search-input** - Type: Input - Field to search venues by name or location.   - **ID: venue-capacity-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by capacity (Small, Medium, Large).   - **ID: view-venue-details-{venue_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view venue details (each venue card has this).  ### 7. Event Schedules Page - **Page Title**: Event Schedules - **Overview**: A page displaying event schedules, timelines, and agenda information. - **Elements**:   - **ID: schedules-page** - Type: Div - Container for the schedules page.   - **ID: schedules-timeline** - Type: Div - Timeline view of upcoming events and sessions.   - **ID: schedule-filter-date** - Type: Input (date) - Field to filter schedules by date.   - **ID: schedule-filter-event** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by event.   - **ID: export-schedule-button** - Type: Button - Button to export schedule data.  ### 8. Bookings Summary Page - **Page Title**: My Bookings - **Overview**: A page displaying all user bookings with ticket information and booking status. - **Elements**:   - **ID: bookings-page** - Type: Div - Container for the bookings page.   - **ID: bookings-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying bookings with event, date, ticket count, and status.   - **ID: booking-search-input** - Type: Input - Field to search bookings by event name or booking ID.   - **ID: cancel-booking-button-{booking_id}** - Type: Button - Button to cancel booking (each booking has this).   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ## 4. Data Storage  The 'EventPlanning' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:  ### 1. Events Data - **File Name**: `events.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   event_id|event_name|category|date|time|location|description|venue_id|capacity   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|Tech Conference 2025|Conference|2025-03-15|09:00|Convention Center, San Francisco|Annual technology conference discussing latest innovations|1|500   2|Summer Music Festival|Concert|2025-06-20|18:00|Central Park, New York|Three-day music festival with international artists|2|5000   3|Marathon Championship|Sports|2025-04-10|07:00|Downtown Loop, Chicago|Annual city marathon event for all skill levels|3|1000   ```  ### 2. Venues Data - **File Name**: `venues.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   venue_id|venue_name|location|capacity|amenities|contact   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|Convention Center|San Francisco, CA|500|WiFi, Parking, Catering|contact@convention.com   2|Central Park|New York, NY|5000|Outdoor Space, Restrooms, Food Vendors|info@centralparkevents.org   3|Downtown Loop|Chicago, IL|1000|Paved Surface, Water Stations, Medical Support|events@downtown.com   ```  ### 3. Tickets Data - **File Name**: `tickets.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   ticket_id|event_id|ticket_type|price|available_count|sold_count   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|1|General|49.99|500|150   2|1|VIP|99.99|100|45   3|2|Early Bird|39.99|1000|750   ```  ### 4. Bookings Data - **File Name**: `bookings.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   booking_id|event_id|customer_name|booking_date|ticket_count|ticket_type|total_amount|status   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|1|Alice Johnson|2025-02-01|2|General|99.98|Confirmed   2|2|Bob Williams|2025-02-05|4|Early Bird|159.96|Confirmed   3|1|Carol Davis|2025-02-10|1|VIP|99.99|Pending   ```  ### 5. Participants Data - **File Name**: `participants.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   participant_id|event_id|name|email|booking_id|status|registration_date   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|1|Alice Johnson|alice@email.com|1|Confirmed|2025-02-01   2|1|Michael Johnson|michael@email.com|1|Confirmed|2025-02-01   3|2|Bob Williams|bob@email.com|2|Attended|2025-02-05   ```  ### 6. Schedules Data - **File Name**: `schedules.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   schedule_id|event_id|session_title|session_time|duration_minutes|speaker|venue_id   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|1|Opening Keynote|2025-03-15 09:00|60|John Smith|1   2|1|Panel Discussion|2025-03-15 10:30|90|Expert Panel|1   3|2|Headliner Performance|2025-06-20 20:00|120|International Artist|2   ```

Dashboard\n- **Route:** `/dashboard`\n- **Methods:** GET\n- **Function:** `dashboard()`\n- **Description:** Render the Dashboard page showing upcoming events, featured venues, and navigation buttons.\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `featured_events` (list of dicts): list of featured event recommendations with keys `event_id`, `event_name`, `date`, `location`, `category`.\n\n#### Template\n- `templates/dashboard.html`\n  - **Page ID:** `dashboard-page`\n  - **Elements:**\n    - Featured events display section.\n    - Button with `id='browse-events-button'` to navigate to `/events`.\n    - Button with `id='tickets-page-button'` to navigate to `/tickets`.\n\n#### Navigation Buttons\n- Browse Events -> `/events`\n- Tickets -> `/tickets`\n\n\n### 2. Events Page\n- **Route:** `/events`\n- **Methods:** GET\n- **Function:** `events()`\n- **Description:** Display a list of events with filter options.\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `events` (list of dicts): each with keys\n    - `event_id` (int)\n    - `event_name` (str)\n    - `category` (str)\n    - `date` (str, YYYY-MM-DD)\n    - `time` (str, HH:MM)\n    - `location` (str)\n  - `categories` (list of str): \n    - e.g. [\"Conference\", \"Sports\", \"Workshop\", \"Social\"]\n  - `filters` (dict): selected filters for name, location, date\n\n#### Template\n- `templates/events.html`\n  - **Page ID:** `events-page`\n  - Div container for event listings: `events-grid`\n  - Filter inputs (name, location, date)\n  - Buttons with IDs `view-event-button-{event_id}` for each listed event.\n\n#### Navigation Buttons\n- Buttons to view event details: `/event/<event_id>`\n\n\n### 3. Event Details Page\n- **Route:** `/event/<int:event_id>`\n- **Methods:** GET\n- **Function:** `event_details(event_id)`\n- **Description:** Show detailed information for a specific event.\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `event` (dict): with keys:\n    - `event_id`, `event_name`, `category`, `date`, `time`, `location`, `description`, `venue_id`, `capacity`\n\n#### Template\n- `templates/event_details.html`\n  - **Page ID:** `event-details-page`\n  - Display fields:\n    - Date: `id='event-date'`\n    - Location: `id='event-location'`\n    - Description: `id='event-description'`\n  - Button `id='book-ticket-button'` to navigate to booking.\n\n#### Navigation Buttons\n- Book Ticket -> `/book_ticket?event_id=<event_id>`\n\n\n### 4. Tickets Page\n- **Route:** `/tickets`\n- **Methods:** GET, POST\n- **Function:** `tickets()`\n- **Description:** Show user ticket bookings and allow booking new tickets.\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `events` (list of dicts): to populate dropdown for event selection.\n  - `bookings` (list of dicts): user's bookings with keys `booking_id`, `event_name`, `date`, `ticket_type`, `quantity`, `status`\n\n#### Template\n- `templates/tickets.html`\n  - **Page ID:** `tickets-page`\n  - Dropdown to select event: `id='event-select'`\n  - Quantity input field: `id='ticket-quantity'`\n  - Dropdown for ticket type (General, Early Bird): `id='ticket-type'`\n  - Button: `id='book-now-button'`\n  - Booking confirmation section: `id='booking-confirmation'`\n\n#### Navigation Buttons\n- POST to submit a booking.\n\n\n### 5. Participants Page\n- **Route:** `/participants`\n- **Methods:** GET, POST\n- **Function:** `participants()`\n- **Description:** Manage event participants, including adding participants and filtering.\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `participants` (list of dicts): with keys `name`, `email`, `event_id`, `status`, `registered_date`\n  - `statuses` (list of str): [\"Registered\", \"Checked In\"]\n  - `filter_status` (str): the currently selected filter\n\n#### Template\n- `templates/participants.html`\n  - **Page ID:** `participants-page`\n  - Container div: `id='participants-container'`\n  - Input to add participant: `id='add-participant-input'`\n  - Filter select: `id='filter-status'`\n\n\n### 6. Venues Page\n- **Route:** `/venues`\n- **Methods:** GET\n- **Function:** `venues()`\n- **Description:** Display venues with filters.\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `venues` (list of dicts): keys:\n    - `venue_id`, `name`, `address`, `facilities` (list), `email`, `capacity` (int)\n  - `capacity_filters` (list of str): [\"Small\", \"Large\"]\n  - `selected_capacity_filter` (str)\n\n#### Template\n- `templates/venues.html`\n  - **Page ID:** `venues-page`\n  - Grid div: `id='venues-grid'`\n  - Input filter: `id='venue-capacity-filter'`\n\n\n### 7. Event Schedules Page\n- **Route:** `/schedules`\n- **Methods:** GET\n- **Function:** `schedules()`\n- **Description:** Display event timelines and allow filtering and exporting.\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `schedules` (list of dicts): keys `start_time`, `duration_minutes`, `description`, `event_id`\n  - `event_filter` (str)\n\n#### Template\n- `templates/schedules.html`\n  - **Page ID:** `schedules-page`\n  - Timeline div: `id='schedules-timeline'`\n  - Input filter: `id='schedule-event-filter'`\n\n\n### 8. My Bookings Page\n- **Route:** `/my_bookings`\n- **Methods:** GET\n- **Function:** `my_bookings()`\n- **Description:** Show the user's bookings with status and allow cancellation.\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `bookings` (list of dicts): keys:\n    - `booking_id`, `event_name`, `date`, `ticket_type`, `quantity`, `status`\n\n#### Template\n- `templates/my_bookings.html`\n  - **Page ID:** `my-bookings-page`\n  - Table of bookings: `id='bookings-table'`\n  - Search input: `id='booking-search'`\n  - Cancel booking button per booking: `id='cancel-booking-button-{booking_id}'`\n  - Refresh button: `id='refresh-button'`\n\n---\n\n## Section Data File Schemas\n\n### 1. events.txt\n- **Path:** `data/events.txt`\n- **Description:** Contains event data.\n- **Format:** pipe-delimited\n\n| Field       | Type   | Description                       |\n|-------------|--------|---------------------------------|\n| event_id    | int    | Unique event identifier          |\n| event_name  | string | Name of the event               |\n| category    | string | Category (Conference, Sports, etc.)|\n| date       | string (YYYY-MM-DD) | Date of event              |\n| time       | string (HH:MM) | Time of event                   |\n| location   | string | Location description             |\n| description | string | Event description               |\n| venue_id   | int    | ID of associated venue           |\n| capacity   | int    | Maximum attendees                |\n\n#### Example Data\n```\n1|Annual Conference|Conference|2025-03-15|09:00|Convention Center, San Francisco|Annual conference with latest tech updates|10|1000\n2|Music Festival|Concert|2025-06-20|18:00|Central Park, New York|Three-day music festival with multiple artists|2|5000\n3|Marathon Championship|Sports|2025-04-10|07:00|Downtown Chicago|Annual marathon event for all runners|5|2000\n```\n\n---\n\n### 2. venues.txt\n- **Path:** `data/venues.txt`\n- **Description:** Venue details.\n- **Format:** pipe-delimited\n\n| Field      | Type    | Description                      |\n|------------|---------|----------------------------------|\n| venue_id   | int     | Unique venue identifier           |\n| name       | string  | Venue name                      |\n| address    | string  | Address                         |\n| facilities | string  | Comma-separated list of facilities|\n| email      | string  | Contact email                   |\n| capacity   | int     | Venue capacity                  |\n\n#### Example Data\n```\n1|Convention Center|123 Market St, San Francisco|Parking,Restrooms,Food Vendors|contact@conventionctr.com|1500\n2|Central Park|Manhattan, New York|Parking,Cafes,Stage|info@centralpark.com|8000\n3|City Stadium|Downtown Chicago|Medical Services,Parking|stadium@citychicago.com|25000\n```\n\n---\n\n### 3. tickets.txt\n- **Path:** `data/tickets.txt`\n- **Description:** Ticket types and pricing.\n- **Format:** pipe-delimited\n\n| Field        | Type         | Description                  |\n|--------------|--------------|------------------------------|\n| ticket_id    | int          | Unique ticket type id         |\n| event_id     | int          | Associated event             |\n| ticket_type  | string       | Type (General, Early Bird)   |\n| price        | float        | Price in USD                 |\n| total_qty    | int          | Total tickets issued          |\n| qty_sold     | int          | Tickets sold                 |\n\n#### Example Data\n```\n1|1|General|49.99|1000|750\n2|2|Early Bird|39.99|1000|300\n3|3|VIP|99.99|500|450\n```\n\n---\n\n### 4. bookings.txt\n- **Path:** `data/bookings.txt`\n- **Description:** User bookings.\n- **Format:** pipe-delimited\n\n| Field        | Type   | Description                  |\n|--------------|--------|------------------------------|\n| booking_id   | int    | Unique booking id             |\n| user_name   | string | User who booked              |\n| booking_date | string | Booking date (YYYY-MM-DD)    |\n| event_id     | int    | Event booked                 |\n| ticket_type  | string | Ticket type                  |\n| total_price  | float  | Total price                  |\n| status       | string | Status (Confirmed, Cancelled)|\n\n#### Example Data\n```\n1|John Williams|2025-02-05|1|Early Bird|159.96|Confirmed\n2|Alice Johnson|2025-03-01|2|General|49.99|Confirmed\n3|Bob Smith|2025-01-20|3|VIP|99.99|Cancelled\n```\n\n---\n\n### 5. participants.txt\n- **Path:** `data/participants.txt`\n- **Description:** Participants registered for events.\n- **Format:** pipe-delimited\n\n| Field         | Type   | Description                   |\n|---------------|--------|-------------------------------|\n| participant_name| string| Name of participant          |\n| email         | string | Email address                |\n| event_id      | int    | Event participated            |\n| status        | string | Registration Events Data - **File Name**: `events.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   event_id|event_name|category|date|time|location|description|venue_id|capacity   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|Tech Conference 2025|Conference|2025-03-15|09:00|Convention Center, San Francisco|Annual technology conference discussing latest innovations|1|500   2|Summer Music Festival|Concert|2025-06-20|18:00|Central Park, New York|Three-day music festival with international artists|2|5000   3|Marathon Championship|Sports|2025-04-10|07:00|Downtown Loop, Chicago|Annual city marathon event for all skill levels|3|1000   ```  ### 2. Venues Data - **File Name**: `venues.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   venue_id|venue_name|location|capacity|amenities|contact   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|Convention Center|San Francisco, CA|500|WiFi, Parking, Catering|contact@convention.com   2|Central Park|New York, NY|5000|Outdoor Space, Restrooms, Food Vendors|info@centralparkevents.org   3|Downtown Loop|Chicago, IL|1000|Paved Surface, Water Stations, Medical Support|events@downtown.com   ```  ### 3. Tickets Data - **File Name**: `tickets.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   ticket_id|event_id|ticket_type|price|available_count|sold_count   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|1|General|49.99|500|150   2|1|VIP|99.99|100|45   3|2|Early Bird|39.99|1000|750   ```  ### 4. Bookings Data - **File Name**: `bookings.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   booking_id|event_id|customer_name|booking_date|ticket_count|ticket_type|total_amount|status   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|1|Alice Johnson|2025-02-01|2|General|99.98|Confirmed   2|2|Bob Williams|2025-02-05|4|Early Bird|159.96|Confirmed   3|1|Carol Davis|2025-02-10|1|VIP|99.99|Pending   ```  ### 5. Participants Data - **File Name**: `participants.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   participant_id|event_id|name|email|booking_id|status|registration_date   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|1|Alice Johnson|alice@email.com|1|Confirmed|2025-02-01   2|1|Michael Johnson|michael@email.com|1|Confirmed|2025-02-01   3|2|Bob Williams|bob@email.com|2|Attended|2025-02-05   ```  ### 6. Schedules Data - **File Name**: `schedules.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   schedule_id|event_id|session_title|session_time|duration_minutes|speaker|venue_id   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|1|Opening Keynote|2025-03-15 09:00|60|John Smith|1   2|1|Panel Discussion|2025-03-15 10:30|90|Expert Panel|1   3|2|Headliner Performance|2025-06-20 20:00|120|International Artist|2   ```
  [design_spec.md] # EventPlanning Flask Application Design Specification  ## Section Routes  ### 1. Dashboard - **Route:** `/dashboard` - **Methods:** GET - **Function:** `dashboard()` - **Description:** Render the Dashboard page showing upcoming events, featured venues, and navigation buttons. - **Context Variables:**   - `featured_events` (list of dicts): list of featured event recommendations with keys `event_id`, `event_name`, `date`, `location`, `category`.  #### Template - `templates/dashboard.html`   - **Page ID:** `dashboard-page`   - **Elements:**     - Featured events display section.     - Button with `id='browse-events-button'` to navigate to `/events`.     - Button with `id='tickets-page-button'` to navigate to `/tickets`.  #### Navigation Buttons - Browse Events -> `/events` - Tickets -> `/tickets`   ### 2. Events Page - **Route:** `/events` - **Methods:** GET - **Function:** `events()` - **Description:** Display a list of events with filter options. - **Context Variables:**   - `events` (list of dicts): each with keys     - `event_id` (int)     - `event_name` (str)     - `category` (str)     - `date` (str, YYYY-MM-DD)     - `time` (str, HH:MM)     - `location` (str)   - `categories` (list of str):      - e.g. ["Conference", "Sports", "Workshop", "Social"]   - `filters` (dict): selected filters for name, location, date  #### Template - `templates/events.html`   - **Page ID:** `events-page`   - Div container for event listings: `events-grid`   - Filter inputs (name, location, date)   - Buttons with IDs `view-event-button-{event_id}` for each listed event.  #### Navigation Buttons - Buttons to view event details: `/event/<event_id>`   ### 3. Event Details Page - **Route:** `/event/<int:event_id>` - **Methods:** GET - **Function:** `event_details(event_id)` - **Description:** Show detailed information for a specific event. - **Context Variables:**   - `event` (dict): with keys:     - `event_id`, `event_name`, `category`, `date`, `time`, `location`, `description`, `venue_id`, `capacity`  #### Template - `templates/event_details.html`   - **Page ID:** `event-details-page`   - Display fields:     - Date: `id='event-date'`     - Location: `id='event-location'`     - Description: `id='event-description'`   - Button `id='book-ticket-button'` to navigate to booking.  #### Navigation Buttons - Book Ticket -> `/book_ticket?event_id=<event_id>`   ### 4. Tickets Page - **Route:** `/tickets` - **Methods:** GET, POST - **Function:** `tickets()` - **Description:** Show user ticket bookings and allow booking new tickets. - **Context Variables:**   - `events` (list of dicts): to populate dropdown for event selection.   - `bookings` (list of dicts): user's bookings with keys `booking_id`, `event_name`, `date`, `ticket_type`, `quantity`, `status`  #### Template - `templates/tickets.html`   - **Page ID:** `tickets-page`   - Dropdown to select event: `id='event-select'`   - Quantity input field: `id='ticket-quantity'`   - Dropdown for ticket type (General, Early Bird): `id='ticket-type'`   - Button: `id='book-now-button'`   - Booking confirmation section: `id='booking-confirmation'`  #### Navigation Buttons - POST to submit a booking.   ### 5. Participants Page - **Route:** `/participants` - **Methods:** GET, POST - **Function:** `participants()` - **Description:** Manage event participants, including adding participants and filtering. - **Context Variables:**   - `participants` (list of dicts): with keys `name`, `email`, `event_id`, `status`, `registered_date`   - `statuses` (list of str): ["Registered", "Checked In"]   - `filter_status` (str): the currently selected filter  #### Template - `templates/participants.html`   - **Page ID:** `participants-page`   - Container div: `id='participants-container'`   - Input to add participant: `id='add-participant-input'`   - Filter select: `id='filter-status'`   ### 6. Venues Page - **Route:** `/venues` - **Methods:** GET - **Function:** `venues()` - **Description:** Display venues with filters. - **Context Variables:**   - `venues` (list of dicts): keys:     - `venue_id`, `name`, `address`, `facilities` (list), `email`, `capacity` (int)   - `capacity_filters` (list of str): ["Small", "Large"]   - `selected_capacity_filter` (str)  #### Template - `templates/venues.html`   - **Page ID:** `venues-page`   - Grid div: `id='venues-grid'`   - Input filter: `id='venue-capacity-filter'`   ### 7. Event Schedules Page - **Route:** `/schedules` - **Methods:** GET - **Function:** `schedules()` - **Description:** Display event timelines and allow filtering and exporting. - **Context Variables:**   - `schedules` (list of dicts): keys `start_time`, `duration_minutes`, `description`, `event_id`   - `event_filter` (str)  #### Template - `templates/schedules.html`   - **Page ID:** `schedules-page`   - Timeline div: `id='schedules-timeline'`   - Input filter: `id='schedule-event-filter'`   ### 8. My Bookings Page - **Route:** `/my_bookings` - **Methods:** GET - **Function:** `my_bookings()` - **Description:** Show the user's bookings with status and allow cancellation. - **Context Variables:**   - `bookings` (list of dicts): keys:     - `booking_id`, `event_name`, `date`, `ticket_type`, `quantity`, `status`  #### Template - `templates/my_bookings.html`   - **Page ID:** `my-bookings-page`   - Table of bookings: `id='bookings-table'`   - Search input: `id='booking-search'`   - Cancel booking button per booking: `id='cancel-booking-button-{booking_id}'`   - Refresh button: `id='refresh-button'`  ---  ## Section Data File Schemas  ### 1. events.txt - **Path:** `data/events.txt` - **Description:** Contains event data. - **Format:** pipe-delimited  | Field       | Type   | Description                       | |-------------|--------|---------------------------------| | event_id    | int    | Unique event identifier          | | event_name  | string | Name of the event               | | category    | string | Category (Conference, Sports, etc.)| | date       | string (YYYY-MM-DD) | Date of event              | | time       | string (HH:MM) | Time of event                   | | location   | string | Location description             | | description | string | Event description               | | venue_id   | int    | ID of associated venue           | | capacity   | int    | Maximum attendees                |  #### Example Data ``` 1|Annual Conference|Conference|2025-03-15|09:00|Convention Center, San Francisco|Annual conference with latest tech updates|10|1000 2|Music Festival|Concert|2025-06-20|18:00|Central Park, New York|Three-day music festival with multiple artists|2|5000 3|Marathon Championship|Sports|2025-04-10|07:00|Downtown Chicago|Annual marathon event for all runners|5|2000 ```  ---  ### 2. venues.txt - **Path:** `data/venues.txt` - **Description:** Venue details. - **Format:** pipe-delimited  | Field      | Type    | Description                      | |------------|---------|----------------------------------| | venue_id   | int     | Unique venue identifier           | | name       | string  | Venue name                      | | address    | string  | Address                         | | facilities | string  | Comma-separated list of facilities| | email      | string  | Contact email                   | | capacity   | int     | Venue capacity                  |  #### Example Data ``` 1|Convention Center|123 Market St, San Francisco|Parking,Restrooms,Food Vendors|contact@conventionctr.com|1500 2|Central Park|Manhattan, New York|Parking,Cafes,Stage|info@centralpark.com|8000 3|City Stadium|Downtown Chicago|Medical Services,Parking|stadium@citychicago.com|25000 ```  ---  ### 3. tickets.txt - **Path:** `data/tickets.txt` - **Description:** Ticket types and pricing. - **Format:** pipe-delimited  | Field        | Type         | Description                  | |--------------|--------------|------------------------------| | ticket_id    | int          | Unique ticket type id         | | event_id     | int          | Associated event             | | ticket_type  | string       | Type (General, Early Bird)   | | price        | float        | Price in USD                 | | total_qty    | int          | Total tickets issued          | | qty_sold     | int          | Tickets sold                 |  #### Example Data ``` 1|1|General|49.99|1000|750 2|2|Early Bird|39.99|1000|300 3|3|VIP|99.99|500|450 ```  ---  ### 4. bookings.txt - **Path:** `data/bookings.txt` - **Description:** User bookings. - **Format:** pipe-delimited  | Field        | Type   | Description                  | |--------------|--------|------------------------------| | booking_id   | int    | Unique booking id             | | user_name   | string | User who booked              | | booking_date | string | Booking date (YYYY-MM-DD)    | | event_id     | int    | Event booked                 | | ticket_type  | string | Ticket type                  | | total_price  | float  | Total price                  | | status       | string | Status (Confirmed, Cancelled)|  #### Example Data ``` 1|John Williams|2025-02-05|1|Early Bird|159.96|Confirmed 2|Alice Johnson|2025-03-01|2|General|49.99|Confirmed 3|Bob Smith|2025-01-20|3|VIP|99.99|Cancelled ```  ---  ### 5. participants.txt - **Path:** `data/participants.txt` - **Description:** Participants registered for events. - **Format:** pipe-delimited  | Field         | Type   | Description                   | |---------------|--------|-------------------------------| | participant_name| string| Name of participant          | | email         | string | Email address                | | event_id      | int    | Event participated            | | status        | string | Registration status           | | registration_date | string | Date of registration          |  #### Example Data ``` Alice Johnson|alice@email.com|1|Confirmed|2025-02-01 Bob Smith|bob@email.com|2|Registered|2025-03-05 Charlie Brown|charlie@email.com|3|Checked In|2025-01-15 ```  ---  ### 6. schedules.txt - **Path:** `data/schedules.txt` - **Description:** Event schedules and timelines. - **Format:** pipe-delimited  | Field          | Type   | Description                   | |----------------|--------|-------------------------------| | start_time     | string | Time (HH:MM)                 | | duration_mins  | int    | Duration in minutes          | | description    | string | Description of schedule item | | event_id       | int    | Associated event             |  #### Example Data ``` 09:00|60|Opening Keynote|1 20:00|120|Main Concert|2 07:00|180|Marathon Race|3 ```   ---  This specification enables complete development of the 'EventPlanning' Flask application including data loading from specified files, route handlers, templates with IDs and context variables.

# Requirements Document for 'EventPlanning' Web Application

## 1. Objective
Develop a comprehensive web application named 'EventPlanning' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to browse events, book tickets, view venue information, manage participants, and explore event schedules. No authentication required - all features are directly accessible. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.

## 2. Language
The required development language for the 'EventPlanning' application is Python.

## 3. Page Design

The 'EventPlanning' web application will consist of the following eight pages:

### 1. Dashboard Page
- **Page Title**: Event Planning Dashboard
- **Overview**: The main hub displaying upcoming events, featured venues, and quick navigation to all functionalities.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.
  - **ID: featured-events** - Type: Div - Display of featured event recommendations.
  - **ID: browse-events-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to events listing page.
  - **ID: view-tickets-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to tickets page.
  - **ID: venues-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to venues page.

### 2. Events Listing Page
- **Page Title**: Events Catalog
- **Overview**: A page displaying all available events with search and filter capabilities.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: events-page** - Type: Div - Container for the events listing page.
  - **ID: event-search-input** - Type: Input - Field to search events by name, location, or date.
  - **ID: event-category-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by category (Conference, Concert, Sports, Workshop, Social).
  - **ID: events-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying event cards with image, title, date, and location.
  - **ID: view-event-button-{event_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view event details (each event card has this).

### 3. Event Details Page
- **Page Title**: Event Details
- **Overview**: A page displaying detailed information about a specific event.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: event-details-page** - Type: Div - Container for the event details page.
  - **ID: event-title** - Type: H1 - Display event title.
  - **ID: event-date** - Type: Div - Display event date and time.
  - **ID: event-location** - Type: Div - Display event location.
  - **ID: event-description** - Type: Div - Display detailed event description.
  - **ID: book-ticket-button** - Type: Button - Button to book ticket for this event.

### 4. Ticket Booking Page
- **Page Title**: Book Your Tickets
- **Overview**: A page for users to select and book tickets for events.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: ticket-booking-page** - Type: Div - Container for the ticket booking page.
  - **ID: select-event-dropdown** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select event to book tickets.
  - **ID: ticket-quantity-input** - Type: Input (number) - Field to enter number of tickets.
  - **ID: ticket-type-select** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select ticket type (General, VIP, Early Bird).
  - **ID: book-now-button** - Type: Button - Button to proceed with ticket booking.
  - **ID: booking-confirmation** - Type: Div - Display booking confirmation details.

### 5. Participants Management Page
- **Page Title**: Participants Management
- **Overview**: A page for managing event participants and attendee lists.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: participants-page** - Type: Div - Container for the participants management page.
  - **ID: participants-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying participants with name, email, event, and status.
  - **ID: add-participant-button** - Type: Button - Button to add new participant.
  - **ID: search-participant-input** - Type: Input - Field to search participants by name or email.
  - **ID: participant-status-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by status (Registered, Confirmed, Attended).

### 6. Venue Information Page
- **Page Title**: Venues
- **Overview**: A page displaying available venues for events with detailed information.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: venues-page** - Type: Div - Container for the venues page.
  - **ID: venues-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying venue cards with name, capacity, and amenities.
  - **ID: venue-search-input** - Type: Input - Field to search venues by name or location.
  - **ID: venue-capacity-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by capacity (Small, Medium, Large).
  - **ID: view-venue-details-{venue_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view venue details (each venue card has this).

### 7. Event Schedules Page
- **Page Title**: Event Schedules
- **Overview**: A page displaying event schedules, timelines, and agenda information.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: schedules-page** - Type: Div - Container for the schedules page.
  - **ID: schedules-timeline** - Type: Div - Timeline view of upcoming events and sessions.
  - **ID: schedule-filter-date** - Type: Input (date) - Field to filter schedules by date.
  - **ID: schedule-filter-event** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by event.
  - **ID: export-schedule-button** - Type: Button - Button to export schedule data.

### 8. Bookings Summary Page
- **Page Title**: My Bookings
- **Overview**: A page displaying all user bookings with ticket information and booking status.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: bookings-page** - Type: Div - Container for the bookings page.
  - **ID: bookings-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying bookings with event, date, ticket count, and status.
  - **ID: booking-search-input** - Type: Input - Field to search bookings by event name or booking ID.
  - **ID: cancel-booking-button-{booking_id}** - Type: Button - Button to cancel booking (each booking has this).
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

## 4. Data Storage

The 'EventPlanning' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:

### 1. Events Data
- **File Name**: `events.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  event_id|event_name|category|date|time|location|description|venue_id|capacity
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|Tech Conference 2025|Conference|2025-03-15|09:00|Convention Center, San Francisco|Annual technology conference discussing latest innovations|1|500
  2|Summer Music Festival|Concert|2025-06-20|18:00|Central Park, New York|Three-day music festival with international artists|2|5000
  3|Marathon Championship|Sports|2025-04-10|07:00|Downtown Loop, Chicago|Annual city marathon event for all skill levels|3|1000
  ```

### 2. Venues Data
- **File Name**: `venues.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  venue_id|venue_name|location|capacity|amenities|contact
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|Convention Center|San Francisco, CA|500|WiFi, Parking, Catering|contact@convention.com
  2|Central Park|New York, NY|5000|Outdoor Space, Restrooms, Food Vendors|info@centralparkevents.org
  3|Downtown Loop|Chicago, IL|1000|Paved Surface, Water Stations, Medical Support|events@downtown.com
  ```

### 3. Tickets Data
- **File Name**: `tickets.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  ticket_id|event_id|ticket_type|price|available_count|sold_count
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|1|General|49.99|500|150
  2|1|VIP|99.99|100|45
  3|2|Early Bird|39.99|1000|750
  ```

### 4. Bookings Data
- **File Name**: `bookings.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  booking_id|event_id|customer_name|booking_date|ticket_count|ticket_type|total_amount|status
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|1|Alice Johnson|2025-02-01|2|General|99.98|Confirmed
  2|2|Bob Williams|2025-02-05|4|Early Bird|159.96|Confirmed
  3|1|Carol Davis|2025-02-10|1|VIP|99.99|Pending
  ```

### 5. Participants Data
- **File Name**: `participants.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  participant_id|event_id|name|email|booking_id|status|registration_date
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|1|Alice Johnson|alice@email.com|1|Confirmed|2025-02-01
  2|1|Michael Johnson|michael@email.com|1|Confirmed|2025-02-01
  3|2|Bob Williams|bob@email.com|2|Attended|2025-02-05
  ```

### 6. Schedules Data
- **File Name**: `schedules.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  schedule_id|event_id|session_title|session_time|duration_minutes|speaker|venue_id
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|1|Opening Keynote|2025-03-15 09:00|60|John Smith|1
  2|1|Panel Discussion|2025-03-15 10:30|90|Expert Panel|1
  3|2|Headliner Performance|2025-06-20 20:00|120|International Artist|2
  ```

# EventPlanning Flask Application Design Specification

## Section Routes

### 1. Dashboard
- **Route:** `/dashboard`
- **Methods:** GET
- **Function:** `dashboard()`
- **Description:** Render the Dashboard page showing upcoming events, featured venues, and navigation buttons.
- **Context Variables:**
  - `featured_events` (list of dicts): list of featured event recommendations with keys `event_id`, `event_name`, `date`, `location`, `category`.

#### Template
- `templates/dashboard.html`
  - **Page ID:** `dashboard-page`
  - **Elements:**
    - Featured events display section.
    - Button with `id='browse-events-button'` to navigate to `/events`.
    - Button with `id='tickets-page-button'` to navigate to `/tickets`.

#### Navigation Buttons
- Browse Events -> `/events`
- Tickets -> `/tickets`


### 2. Events Page
- **Route:** `/events`
- **Methods:** GET
- **Function:** `events()`
- **Description:** Display a list of events with filter options.
- **Context Variables:**
  - `events` (list of dicts): each with keys
    - `event_id` (int)
    - `event_name` (str)
    - `category` (str)
    - `date` (str, YYYY-MM-DD)
    - `time` (str, HH:MM)
    - `location` (str)
  - `categories` (list of str): 
    - e.g. ["Conference", "Sports", "Workshop", "Social"]
  - `filters` (dict): selected filters for name, location, date

#### Template

- **Methods:** GET
- **Function:** `my_bookings()`
- **Description:** Show the user's bookings with status and allow cancellation.
- **Context Variables:**
  - `bookings` (list of dicts): keys:
    - `booking_id`, `event_name`, `date`, `ticket_type`, `quantity`, `status`

#### Template
- `templates/my_bookings.html`
  - **Page ID:** `my-bookings-page`
  - Table of bookings: `id='bookings-table'`
  - Search input: `id='booking-search'`
  - Cancel booking button per booking: `id='cancel-booking-button-{booking_id}'`
  - Refresh button: `id='refresh-button'`

---

## Section Data File Schemas

### 1. events.txt
- **Path:** `data/events.txt`
- **Description:** Contains event data.
- **Format:** pipe-delimited

| Field       | Type   | Description                       |
|-------------|--------|---------------------------------|
| event_id    | int    | Unique event identifier          |
| event_name  | string | Name of the event               |
| category    | string | Category (Conference, Sports, etc.)|
| date       | string (YYYY-MM-DD) | Date of event              |
| time       | string (HH:MM) | Time of event                   |
| location   | string | Location description             |
| description | string | Event description               |
| venue_id   | int    | ID of associated venue           |
| capacity   | int    | Maximum attendees                |

#### Example Data
```
1|Annual Conference|Conference|2025-03-15|09:00|Convention Center, San Francisco|Annual conference with latest tech updates|10|1000
2|Music Festival|Concert|2025-06-20|18:00|Central Park, New York|Three-day music festival with multiple artists|2|5000
3|Marathon Championship|Sports|2025-04-10|07:00|Downtown Chicago|Annual marathon event for all runners|5|2000
```

---

### 2. venues.txt
- **Path:** `data/venues.txt`
- **Description:** Venue details.
- **Format:** pipe-delimited

| Field      | Type    | Description                      |
|------------|---------|----------------------------------|
| venue_id   | int     | Unique venue identifier           |
| name       | string  | Venue name                      |
| address    | string  | Address                         |
| facilities | string  | Comma-separated list of facilities|
| email      | string  | Contact email                   |
| capacity   | int     | Venue capacity                  |

#### Example Data
```
1|Convention Center|123 Market St, San Francisco|Parking,Restrooms,Food Vendors|contact@conventionctr.com|1500
2|Central Park|Manhattan, New York|Parking,Cafes,Stage|info@centralpark.com|8000
3|City Stadium|Downtown Chicago|Medical Services,Parking|stadium@citychicago.com|25000
```

---

### 3. tickets.txt
- **Path:** `data/tickets.txt`
- **Description:** Ticket types and pricing.
- **Format:** pipe-delimited

| Field        | Type         | Description                  |
|--------------|--------------|------------------------------|
| ticket_id    | int          | Unique ticket type id         |
| event_id     | int          | Associated event             |
| ticket_type  | string       | Type (General, Early Bird)   |
| price        | float        | Price in USD                 |
| total_qty    | int          | Total tickets issued          |
| qty_sold     | int          | Tickets sold                 |

#### Example Data
```
1|1|General|49.99|1000|750
2|2|Early Bird|39.99|1000|300
3|3|VIP|99.99|500|450
```

---

### 4. bookings.txt
- **Path:** `data/bookings.txt`
- **Description:** User bookings.
- **Format:** pipe-delimited

| Field        | Type   | Description                  |
|--------------|--------|------------------------------|
| booking_id   | int    | Unique booking id             |
| user_name   | string | User who booked              |
| booking_date | string | Booking date (YYYY-MM-DD)    |
| event_id     | int    | Event booked                 |
| ticket_type  | string | Ticket type                  |
| total_price  | float  | Total price                  |
| status       | string | Status (Confirmed, Cancelled)|

#### Example Data
```
1|John Williams|2025-02-05|1|Early Bird|159.96|Confirmed
2|Alice Johnson|2025-03-01|2|General|49.99|Confirmed
3|Bob Smith|2025-01-20|3|VIP|99.99|Cancelled
```

---

### 5. participants.txt
- **Path:** `data/participants.txt`
- **Description:** Participants registered for events.
- **Format:** pipe-delimited

| Field         | Type   | Description                   |
|---------------|--------|-------------------------------|
| participant_name| string| Name of participant          |
| email         | string | Email address                |
| event_id      | int    | Event participated            |
| status        | string | Registration status           |
| registration_date | string | Date of registration          |

#### Example Data
```
Alice Johnson|alice@email.com|1|Confirmed|2025-02-01
Bob Smith|bob@email.com|2|Registered|2025-03-05
Charlie Brown|charlie@email.com|3|Checked In|2025-01-15
```

---

### 6. schedules.txt
- **Path:** `data/schedules.txt`
- **Description:** Event schedules and timelines.
- **Format:** pipe-delimited

| Field          | Type   | Description                   |
|----------------|--------|-------------------------------|
| start_time     | string | Time (HH:MM)                 |
| duration_mins  | int    | Duration in minutes          |
| description    | string | Description of schedule item |
| event_id       | int    | Associated event             |

#### Example Data
```
09:00|60|Opening Keynote|1
20:00|120|Main Concert|2
07:00|180|Marathon Race|3
```

  [user_task_description] # Requirements Document for 'EventPlanning' Web Application  ## 1. Objective Develop a comprehensive web application named 'EventPlanning' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to browse events, book tickets, view venue information, manage participants, and explore event schedules. No authentication required - all features are directly accessible. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.  ## 2. Language The required development language for the 'EventPlanning' application is Python.  ## 3. Page Design  The 'EventPlanning' web application will consist of the following eight pages:  ### 1. Dashboard Page - **Page Title**: Event Planning Dashboard - **Overview**: The main hub displaying upcoming events, featured venues, and quick navigation to all functionalities. - **Elements**:   - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.   - **ID: featured-events** - Type: Div - Display of featured event recommendations.   - **ID: browse-events-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to events listing page.   - **ID: view-tickets-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to tickets page.   - **ID: venues-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to venues page.  ### 2. Events Listing Page - **Page Title**: Events Catalog - **Overview**: A page displaying all available events with search and filter capabilities. - **Elements**:   - **ID: events-page** - Type: Div - Container for the events listing page.   - **ID: event-search-input** - Type: Input - Field to search events by name, location, or date.   - **ID: event-category-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by category (Conference, Concert, Sports, Workshop, Social).   - **ID: events-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying event cards with image, title, date, and location.   - **ID: view-event-button-{event_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view event details (each event card has this).  ### 3. Event Details Page - **Page Title**: Event Details - **Overview**: A page displaying detailed information about a specific event. - **Elements**:   - **ID: event-details-page** - Type: Div - Container for the event details page.   - **ID: event-title** - Type: H1 - Display event title.   - **ID: event-date** - Type: Div - Display event date and time.   - **ID: event-location** - Type: Div - Display event location.   - **ID: event-description** - Type: Div - Display detailed event description.   - **ID: book-ticket-button** - Type: Button - Button to book ticket for this event.  ### 4. Ticket Booking Page - **Page Title**: Book Your Tickets - **Overview**: A page for users to select and book tickets for events. - **Elements**:   - **ID: ticket-booking-page** - Type: Div - Container for the ticket booking page.   - **ID: select-event-dropdown** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select event to book tickets.   - **ID: ticket-quantity-input** - Type: Input (number) - Field to enter number of tickets.   - **ID: ticket-type-select** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select ticket type (General, VIP, Early Bird).   - **ID: book-now-button** - Type: Button - Button to proceed with ticket booking.   - **ID: booking-confirmation** - Type: Div - Display booking confirmation details.  ### 5. Participants Management Page - **Page Title**: Participants Management - **Overview**: A page for managing event participants and attendee lists. - **Elements**:   - **ID: participants-page** - Type: Div - Container for the participants management page.   - **ID: participants-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying participants with name, email, event, and status.   - **ID: add-participant-button** - Type: Button - Button to add new participant.   - **ID: search-participant-input** - Type: Input - Field to search participants by name or email.   - **ID: participant-status-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by status (Registered, Confirmed, Attended).  ### 6. Venue Information Page - **Page Title**: Venues - **Overview**: A page displaying available venues for events with detailed information. - **Elements**:   - **ID: venues-page** - Type: Div - Container for the venues page.   - **ID: venues-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying venue cards with name, capacity, and amenities.   - **ID: venue-search-input** - Type: Input - Field to search venues by name or location.   - **ID: venue-capacity-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by capacity (Small, Medium, Large).   - **ID: view-venue-details-{venue_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view venue details (each venue card has this).  ### 7. Event Schedules Page - **Page Title**: Event Schedules - **Overview**: A page displaying event schedules, timelines, and agenda information. - **Elements**:   - **ID: schedules-page** - Type: Div - Container for the schedules page.   - **ID: schedules-timeline** - Type: Div - Timeline view of upcoming events and sessions.   - **ID: schedule-filter-date** - Type: Input (date) - Field to filter schedules by date.   - **ID: schedule-filter-event** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by event.   - **ID: export-schedule-button** - Type: Button - Button to export schedule data.  ### 8. Bookings Summary Page - **Page Title**: My Bookings - **Overview**: A page displaying all user bookings with ticket information and booking status. - **Elements**:   - **ID: bookings-page** - Type: Div - Container for the bookings page.   - **ID: bookings-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying bookings with event, date, ticket count, and status.   - **ID: booking-search-input** - Type: Input - Field to search bookings by event name or booking ID.   - **ID: cancel-booking-button-{booking_id}** - Type: Button - Button to cancel booking (each booking has this).   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ## 4. Data Storage  The 'EventPlanning' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:  ### 1. Events Data - **File Name**: `events.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   event_id|event_name|category|date|time|location|description|venue_id|capacity   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|Tech Conference 2025|Conference|2025-03-15|09:00|Convention Center, San Francisco|Annual technology conference discussing latest innovations|1|500   2|Summer Music Festival|Concert|2025-06-20|18:00|Central Park, New York|Three-day music festival with international artists|2|5000   3|Marathon Championship|Sports|2025-04-10|07:00|Downtown Loop, Chicago|Annual city marathon event for all skill levels|3|1000   ```  ### 2. Venues Data - **File Name**: `venues.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   venue_id|venue_name|location|capacity|amenities|contact   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|Convention Center|San Francisco, CA|500|WiFi, Parking, Catering|contact@convention.com   2|Central Park|New York, NY|5000|Outdoor Space, Restrooms, Food Vendors|info@centralparkevents.org   3|Downtown Loop|Chicago, IL|1000|Paved Surface, Water Stations, Medical Support|events@downtown.com   ```  ### 3. Tickets Data - **File Name**: `tickets.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   ticket_id|event_id|ticket_type|price|available_count|sold_count   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|1|General|49.99|500|150   2|1|VIP|99.99|100|45   3|2|Early Bird|39.99|1000|750   ```  ### 4. Bookings Data - **File Name**: `bookings.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   booking_id|event_id|customer_name|booking_date|ticket_count|ticket_type|total_amount|status   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|1|Alice Johnson|2025-02-01|2|General|99.98|Confirmed   2|2|Bob Williams|2025-02-05|4|Early Bird|159.96|Confirmed   3|1|Carol Davis|2025-02-10|1|VIP|99.99|Pending   ```  ### 5. Participants Data - **File Name**: `participants.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   participant_id|event_id|name|email|booking_id|status|registration_date   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|1|Alice Johnson|alice@email.com|1|Confirmed|2025-02-01   2|1|Michael Johnson|michael@email.com|1|Confirmed|2025-02-01   3|2|Bob Williams|bob@email.com|2|Attended|2025-02-05   ```  ### 6. Schedules Data - **File Name**: `schedules.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   schedule_id|event_id|session_title|session_time|duration_minutes|speaker|venue_id   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|1|Opening Keynote|2025-03-15 09:00|60|John Smith|1   2|1|Panel Discussion|2025-03-15 10:30|90|Expert Panel|1   3|2|Headliner Performance|2025-06-20 20:00|120|International Artist|2   ```
  [design_spec.md] # EventPlanning Flask Application Design Specification  ## Section Routes  ### 1. Dashboard - **Route:** `/dashboard` - **Methods:** GET - **Function:** `dashboard()` - **Description:** Render the Dashboard page showing upcoming events, featured venues, and navigation buttons. - **Context Variables:**   - `featured_events` (list of dicts): list of featured event recommendations with keys `event_id`, `event_name`, `date`, `location`, `category`.  #### Template - `templates/dashboard.html`   - **Page ID:** `dashboard-page`   - **Elements:**     - Featured events display section.     - Button with `id='browse-events-button'` to navigate to `/events`.     - Button with `id='tickets-page-button'` to navigate to `/tickets`.  #### Navigation Buttons - Browse Events -> `/events` - Tickets -> `/tickets`   ### 2. Events Page - **Route:** `/events` - **Methods:** GET - **Function:** `events()` - **Description:** Display a list of events with filter options. - **Context Variables:**   - `events` (list of dicts): each with keys     - `event_id` (int)     - `event_name` (str)     - `category` (str)     - `date` (str, YYYY-MM-DD)     - `time` (str, HH:MM)     - `location` (str)   - `categories` (list of str):      - e.g. ["Conference", "Sports", "Workshop", "Social"]   - `filters` (dict): selected filters for name, location, date  #### Template - `templates/events.html`   - **Page ID:** `events-page`   - Div container for event listings: `events-grid`   - Filter inputs (name, location, date)   - Buttons with IDs `view-event-button-{event_id}` for each listed event.  #### Navigation Buttons - Buttons to view event details: `/event/<event_id>`   ### 3. Event Details Page - **Route:** `/event/<int:event_id>` - **Methods:** GET - **Function:** `event_details(event_id)` - **Description:** Show detailed information for a specific event. - **Context Variables:**   - `event` (dict): with keys:     - `event_id`, `event_name`, `category`, `date`, `time`, `location`, `description`, `venue_id`, `capacity`  #### Template - `templates/event_details.html`   - **Page ID:** `event-details-page`   - Display fields:     - Date: `id='event-date'`     - Location: `id='event-location'`     - Description: `id='event-description'`   - Button `id='book-ticket-button'` to navigate to booking.  #### Navigation Buttons - Book Ticket -> `/book_ticket?event_id=<event_id>`   ### 4. Tickets Page - **Route:** `/tickets` - **Methods:** GET, POST - **Function:** `tickets()` - **Description:** Show user ticket bookings and allow booking new tickets. - **Context Variables:**   - `events` (list of dicts): to populate dropdown for event selection.   - `bookings` (list of dicts): user's bookings with keys `booking_id`, `event_name`, `date`, `ticket_type`, `quantity`, `status`  #### Template - `templates/tickets.html`   - **Page ID:** `tickets-page`   - Dropdown to select event: `id='event-select'`   - Quantity input field: `id='ticket-quantity'`   - Dropdown for ticket type (General, Early Bird): `id='ticket-type'`   - Button: `id='book-now-button'`   - Booking confirmation section: `id='booking-confirmation'`  #### Navigation Buttons - POST to submit a booking.   ### 5. Participants Page - **Route:** `/participants` - **Methods:** GET, POST - **Function:** `participants()` - **Description:** Manage event participants, including adding participants and filtering. - **Context Variables:**   - `participants` (list of dicts): with keys `name`, `email`, `event_id`, `status`, `registered_date`   - `statuses` (list of str): ["Registered", "Checked In"]   - `filter_status` (str): the currently selected filter  #### Template - `templates/participants.html`   - **Page ID:** `participants-page`   - Container div: `id='participants-container'`   - Input to add participant: `id='add-participant-input'`   - Filter select: `id='filter-status'`   ### 6. Venues Page - **Route:** `/venues` - **Methods:** GET - **Function:** `venues()` - **Description:** Display venues with filters. - **Context Variables:**   - `venues` (list of dicts): keys:     - `venue_id`, `name`, `address`, `facilities` (list), `email`, `capacity` (int)   - `capacity_filters` (list of str): ["Small", "Large"]   - `selected_capacity_filter` (str)  #### Template - `templates/venues.html`   - **Page ID:** `venues-page`   - Grid div: `id='venues-grid'`   - Input filter: `id='venue-capacity-filter'`   ### 7. Event Schedules Page - **Route:** `/schedules` - **Methods:** GET - **Function:** `schedules()` - **Description:** Display event timelines and allow filtering and exporting. - **Context Variables:**   - `schedules` (list of dicts): keys `start_time`, `duration_minutes`, `description`, `event_id`   - `event_filter` (str)  #### Template - `templates/schedules.html`   - **Page ID:** `schedules-page`   - Timeline div: `id='schedules-timeline'`   - Input filter: `id='schedule-event-filter'`   ### 8. My Bookings Page - **Route:** `/my_bookings` - **Methods:** GET - **Function:** `my_bookings()` - **Description:** Show the user's bookings with status and allow cancellation. - **Context Variables:**   - `bookings` (list of dicts): keys:     - `booking_id`, `event_name`, `date`, `ticket_type`, `quantity`, `status`  #### Template - `templates/my_bookings.html`   - **Page ID:** `my-bookings-page`   - Table of bookings: `id='bookings-table'`   - Search input: `id='booking-search'`   - Cancel booking button per booking: `id='cancel-booking-button-{booking_id}'`   - Refresh button: `id='refresh-button'`  ---  ## Section Data File Schemas  ### 1. events.txt -
